\"text\": \"## Grafana Configuration Loading System - Complete Analysis\\n\\nGrafana's configuration system is a comprehensive multi-layer override chain implemented in the `pkg/setting` package. The main entry point is `NewCfgFromArgs()` in `pkg/setting/setting.go:1156`, which calls `Load()` to initialize the configuration.\\n\\n### Configuration Loading Chain (Order of Precedence)\\n\\nThe configuration is loaded and applied in the following order (lowest to highest precedence):\\n\\n1. **Defaults (conf/defaults.ini)**: The base configuration file located at `conf/defaults.ini` is loaded first via `ini.Load()` at `pkg/setting/setting.go:1039`.\\n\\n2. **Command-Line Default Properties**: Applied via `applyCommandLineDefaultProperties()` at line 1049, which parses the `cfg:` command-line arguments.\\n\\n3. **Custom Configuration File**: Loaded via `loadSpecifiedConfigFile()` at line 1052, which by default looks for `conf/custom.ini` but can be overridden with the `--config` parameter.\\n\\n4. **Environment Variable Overrides**: Applied via `applyEnvVariableOverrides()` at line 1063, which checks for environment variables matching the pattern `GF_SECTION_KEY` (created by `EnvKey()` at line 919).\\n\\n5. **Command-Line Properties**: Applied via `applyCommandLineProperties()` at line 1069, using the same `cfg:` syntax as command-line default properties.\\n\\n6. **Configuration Value Expansion**: Performed via `expandConfig()` from `pkg/setting/expanders.go:52`, which expands environment variable patterns within configuration values using the syntax `${VAR}` or `$__file{path}`.\\n\\n### INI File Parsing\\n\\nThe INI parsing is done using the `gopkg.in/ini.v1` library. The `loadConfiguration()` function orchestrates the loading:\\n- Loads the INI file using `ini.Load()` at line 1039\\n- Merges sections and keys from additional config files\\n- Each key-value pair is accessible via `ini.File.Section().Key()` methods\\n\\n### Environment Variable Override Logic\\n\\nThe `applyEnvVariableOverrides()` function (line 806) implements the environment variable override mechanism:\\n- Iterates through all sections and keys in the INI file\\n- For each key, constructs an environment variable name using `EnvKey(sectionName, keyName)` which produces names like `GF_DATABASE_URL` or `GF_AUTH_GOOGLE_ENABLED`\\n- If an environment variable exists with that name, its value overrides the configuration value\\n- The applied overrides are tracked in `cfg.appliedEnvOverrides` for logging purposes\\n\\n### Sensitive Value Masking\\n\\nThe `RedactedValue()` function (line 722) masks sensitive configuration values:\\n- Checks if a configuration key matches patterns for sensitive information: PASSWORD, SECRET, PROVIDER_CONFIG, PRIVATE_KEY, SECRET_KEY, CERTIFICATE, ACCOUNT_KEY, ENCRYPTION_KEY, VAULT_TOKEN, CLIENT_SECRET, ENTERPRISE_LICENSE, API_DB_PASS, and token-related keys (with regex support for TOKEN, ID_FORWARDING_TOKEN, AUTHENTICATION_TOKEN, AUTH_TOKEN, RENDERER_TOKEN, API_TOKEN, WEBHOOK_TOKEN, INSTALL_TOKEN)\\n- For sensitive keys, returns `RedactedPassword` constant (value: `\\\"*********\\\"`)\\n- Has exceptions for keys containing RUDDERSTACK, APPLICATION_INSIGHTS, or SENTRY (not masked even if they contain PASSWORD)\\n- For non-sensitive keys containing URLs, applies `RedactedURL()` which masks credentials in URLs\\n- The masking is applied in the settings provider's `Current()` method (provider.go:118-129) which calls `RedactedValue(EnvKey(...), value)` for each setting before returning them to API clients\\n\\n### API Endpoint for Settings (Sensitive Masking)\\n\\nThe `/api/admin/settings` endpoint is implemented in `pkg/api/admin.go:29` with the `AdminGetSettings()` function:\\n- Calls `hs.SettingsProvider.Current()` which returns a `SettingsBag` (map of section
